### Reverts

* "feat(entities): store images as IDs, not plain objects ([#557](https://github.com/webiny/webiny-js/issues/557))" ([#559](https://github.com/webiny/webiny-js/issues/559)) ([fcc7a53](https://github.com/webiny/webiny-js/commit/fcc7a537daadb1f486befa4ffb83c5a0853e4b55))


### BREAKING CHANGES

* This update changes the format of SSR handler response.
* We're now using cursor pagination, which means we no longer have a page and perPage parameters, but rather a "limit" and "after" + "before" cursors.
